<Pictures>None< /Pictures><user_id>102764110545836087939<//user_id>< Review>
With a combination of high premiums and unsatisfactory customer service with our previous auto insurance company, my wife and I were very disappointed and frustrated and we decided to make a change. Upon soliciting quotes from various insurance firms, it was readily apparent that GEICO was (head and shoulder) the best in terms of several metrics including providing the most cost-competitive pricing structure and getting the most "bang for the buck" with respect to the cost/benefit ratio.However, and while it was easy to measure and evaluate this (pricing/premium) metric, we were not 100% certain about GEICO's customer service performance. After being a member with GEICO now for more than a month (and having several opportunities to test and evaluate their performance), I can unequivocally and categorically state that GEIGO is the best insurance company in San Diego. We can attest to that because we've been with several insurance firms within the past 20 years, and (in our judgment) GEICO sets the gold standard.Frankly, and since my wife and I come from the "old school", we value relationships and good customer service. GEICO did not disappoint in this "all important" category. Starting with their local manager, Marwa Sayegh, she's very competent, knowledgeable, friendly, respectful, polite, calm, caring and a consummate professional. We found Marwa and her staff (including, in particular, Jay Yarborough and Aaron Zazzera) to be very customer-centric and she's a very good listener and deeply cares about her clients and "goes beyond the call of duty" to ensure complete customer satisfaction. She's simply FANTASTIC.We are very pleased with Marwa and her team at GEICO and we highly recommend them to anyone in need of the best customer service at the most cost-efficient price. By the way, and as a bonus, we were so pleased with Marwa and her team in connection with their superior auto policy that they helped customize for us, we decided to purchase our Homeowner's Insurance Policy with a JV affiliate of GEICO.Therefore, we are very proud and honored to give Marwa and her team a "5" Star Performance Review. Keep up the good work and we hope to be with you and your team for the long-haul...Thank you, John Daiza<//Review>

<date>1608882783395< /date><Rate>4< /Rate>< Review>
I keep hearing about this fried chicken gas station, so yesterday I made it a point to get off the Freeway and stop at Krispy Krunchy Chicken on 14th Street while driving through San Leandro. I've read the Yelp listings and this chain's reviews do not have dining areas and only take out joints. The place was sketchy, but the store was tidy and organized.

Since the batter is thick and floury, the chicken is billed as Krispy. The coating is fine with seasonings, but BBQ, Honey Mustard, House Original, and the best Crystals Hot Sauce have a selection of dipping sauces. On the inside, the chicken is juicy. It's better than dark (white meat). He only had the chicken and none of the other things were available.

With other fast food fried chicken restaurants, prices are on par. The places are not in pleasant neighbourhoods, and crumbs are everywhere if you eat in the car. Minus star for just taking out.<//Review>

< review>
Their $5 chicken tenders weekday lunch special hits the spot! You get 3 chicken tenders, seasoned potato wedges and a honey biscuit. The tenders are just that, tender AND delicious and the wedges are always cooked to perfection, never undercooked and hard. The biscuit rounds out the taste spectrum nicely. The only reason I didn't give them 5 stars is because a dipping sauce doesn't come with the meal. If you want any sauces, they are an additional 0.50c each. Still, it is excellent value for a quick weekday lunch. They also have the Frazil ice drinks which you must try if you haven't already. They are available in 12oz, 20oz and 32oz; 32oz is $3.69 which to this frugal (read: cheapskate) lady is a little pricey but it's enough for 2 to share and the mango is the best mango flavor I think I've ever had! Overall this is one of my favs!< /review>

This is a recently opened pet food store in the beautiful new Los Olivos shopping center. The staff are incredible, they have knowledge about their products and the companies who make them. Their store is immaculately kept and incredibly easy to navigate. If you have been driving to some of the other far off destinations you will not have to do that anymore as they also offer price matching. Next time you need pet food or supplies in Irvine stop in and check out Pet Market you will not be disappointed with their incredible service and quality products.

<Review>Our favorite sushi restaurant in all of San Francisco East Bay Area (Marin County Favorite would be: Sushi Ren).

Anyway, Island Sushi is small, quaint, but a personable experience for us two when we get the sushi craving and want to spend our time in Orinda.  Great Service, good prices (under $100 for 2 with beers and saki), but can order a Bento-Box (soup, salad, rice, 3 additional items for $19.95; or 2 items for $16.95).  Very favorable sushi, lots of options to choose from (Udon, Donburi, multi-entrees, Nigiri, sashimi, Hans rolls, Mali classic rolls), to where the chefs will make up non-menu authentic sushi for us on request, and we treat the chefs to some saki.

Just across the street from Orinda Movie Theatre, pub brew place with some weekend music, Lordes Ice Cream (won't tell you our ‘fav’ ice cream because they may run out when we visit)....great spot for an intimate date.

We visit Sushi Island at least once a month, and we did cheat and tried the sushi restaurant near the pub brew place, but we return back to island sushi because of the more personable experience.</Review><pics>None</pics>< response>
